I called at exactly 9 a.m. when the shop opened to make an appointment. I asked for the best time  as I had multiple people in my party. I was given a time and showed on time for the appointment. Waited thirty minutes before they started one person in the party. Overall it was a three hour ordeal. Helen was very nice and there is a sweet elderly lady who was exceptionally nice however, the manager or owner was the complete opposite. She was rude and curt. When asked about an additional.50 charge she rudely answered saying it was a fee for using a card. Generally information offered and not solicited after it has been charged. Overall, I do NOT recommend this shop unless you want to wait for an extensive period of time and be ridiculously mistreated. Two stars is a little generous considering the experience.< /review>

< text>
I came here a little skeptical after reading some of the reviews. I'm a perfectionist when it comes to nails and when it comes to customer service.

First I called the place to check their hours because it was Labor Day holiday, the lady who answered the phone was very polite and said they had time to do my nails. When I arrived (1.5 hours before closing) they were very friend, I asked to have gel polish and a pedicure. It crossed my mind that the service may be rushed because it was close to closing time, thankfully that was not the case. I had the gel polish on my nails, perfectly applied. I check corners, bubbles etc. It was great. My pedicure was great, they did a great job filing, scrubbing and all that good stuff. To top it off, I had a decent massage! Because I received such great service I decided to ask if they could wax my eyebrows, they were happy to do it! At this point we were almost at closing hours, Lilly waxed my eyebrows and also did a great job. Overall- great experience, great service. I WILL be back and I do recommend. Keep in mind that I am very selective as I mentioned but I always have realistic expectations. :)</text>

< Review>
My boyfriend & I wanted to go get our FEET done. Reading couple reviews before hand, made me second guess trying this place out.
However I used to come to this place waaaay when I was younger, under different management. & decided to go back to see for myself.
We walked in, & we were greeted right away.
It wasnt an upclose interaction but they acknowledged us & was able to take us right away being as Walk-Ins.
As I am sitting in the pedicure massage chairs. This place looks pretty clean, the furniture was comfortable, looked in good shape, no rips and had decent prices for the services provided.
The ladies noticed I am pregnant so I could not enjoy the massage chair. They were gentle with me during the hand massages throughtout my session to not hit a nerve that could affect my pregnancy.  But my boyfriend was able to experience allll the perks that came along with the service we decided on.
Ofcourse he didnt get any color. But him walking on his feet 10 hours, 5 days out of the week. This service did him justice. Feels like a brand new foot! I went for the classic french white tips. I have no cuts. No scratches. No chips. My nails are not too short. I am quite satisfied with my service. She really did a good job, we would definitely go back there.<//Review>

< Review>
They sell mulch, compost, and wood chips at a very reasonable price.  You will need a pickup or trailer as everything is sold in bulk by the cubic yard.  My compact pickup holds 1 cubic yard.  Bring a tarp to keep the mulch from blowing away on your way home.  If you need a large amount, they will deliver for a fee.   They also take greenery from your yard, such as tree and bush trimmings.

The staff is very friendly and helpful and I always enjoy going there.  There is a milk dairy next door so you can take a minute to check out the cows.  BTW, they are closed Saturdays and Sundays.<//Review>

1509291445141< /Time>
<Rating>5< /Rating>< Review>
Shan-e- Punjab is an awesome place. It's basically an Indian grocery store that has a restaurant inside. The grocery store has all the normal amenities like bulk grains and spices. The restaurant seating area is not large, but it's big enough and kind of secluded from the groceries if you want to stop in for a bite.
What makes this place is the food in the restaurant. The quality is very high and the traffic proves it. It gets very busy towards dinner time with both dine in and take out. In fact, quality is so high on the priority list that there are dishes they flat out won't make if they can't get a batch of quality spices in to make it.
From what I understand, Shan-e- actually supplies allot of the local Indian restaurants with product for their kitchens. So if you want it straight from the supplier from amazing chefs then check this place out. You won't be disappointed!</Review>

A few suggestions for the Oakridge Apple Store:

1) Before you nonchalantly ask a customer, "what's your password?", remind them that their private data could be seen and used by others, including Apple employees. Ask them whether they've encrypted their hard drive. And give them the option to erase their hard drives themselves. You are the experts, so inform your customers. You can't expect barbers, truck drivers, doctors, and plumbers to know about data theft, FileVault encryption, two-step verification, computer fraud, and other security issues. Tell corporate to update your training if you have to. We live in an era of government mass surveillance, data mining, financial fraud, and FBI/CIA overreach, so it's up to all of us to keep our data safe.

2) Call back when you say you'll call back. Follow through on your words.

3) It shouldn't take 2-3 weeks for the AppleCare warehouse to find a hard drive that took them 2 days to fix. If it takes that long, then there is a problem with inventory control and supply chain management. Call them and push them to perform. Escalate issues all the way up to management if you have to. Change starts from within!

Just be more professional overall. You are the face of Apple Inc, so try your utmost to represent them well.</Review>
